\KeywordTok{View}\NormalTok{(novocancro)}
\NormalTok{CANCRO<-}\KeywordTok{gather}\NormalTok{(novocancro,}\StringTok{"Year"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"cancer"}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{4}\OperatorTok{:}\DecValTok{17}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{Sex<-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Females"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Males"}\NormalTok{), }\DataTypeTok{times =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{63504}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{63504}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{CANCRO<-}\KeywordTok{cbind}\NormalTok{(CANCRO,Sex)}

\NormalTok{CANCRO}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Year<-}\KeywordTok{sub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Females"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, CANCRO}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Year) }\CommentTok{#Tirar a palavra Females dos anos}
\NormalTok{CANCRO}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Year<-}\KeywordTok{sub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Males"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, CANCRO}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Year) }\CommentTok{#Tirar a palavra Males dos anos}
\NormalTok{CANCRO}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Year<-}\KeywordTok{sub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"."}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, CANCRO}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{Year) }\CommentTok{#Tirar o underscore dos anos}

\NormalTok{CANCRO <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{na.omit}\NormalTok{(CANCRO) }\CommentTok{#NO ENVIRONMENT NAO APARECE AS OBSERVACOES CERTAS}


\NormalTok{CANCRO<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{CANCRO[CANCRO}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CancerSite}\OperatorTok{==}\StringTok{"Bladder"}\NormalTok{,]}
\KeywordTok{View}\NormalTok{(CANCRO)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
